private university based in Berlin, Germany, accredited by the state and the German Science Council. It prepares exceptional students for leadership positions in government, business, and civil society. Interdisciplinary and practice-oriented teaching, first-class research and an extensive international network set the Hertie School apart and position it as an ambassador of good governance, characterised by public debate and engagement. The school was founded at the end of 2003 as a project of the Hertie Foundation, which remains its major partner.<br><strong>Understand today. Shape tomorrow.</strong>\n\t\t</div>\n<div class=\"boilerplate-logo\"><a href=\"/en/\" class=\"logo-link\"><span class=\"label\">Hertie School of Governance</span> <img
